class=\"entry-author\" itemprop=\"author\" itemscope itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Person\"><a href=\"https://gopthedailydose.com/author/harry-hibbs/\" class=\"entry-author-link\" itemprop=\"url\" rel=\"author\"><span class=\"entry-author-name\" itemprop=\"name\">Harry Hibbs</span></a></span> <span class=\"entry-comments-link\"><a href=\"https://gopthedailydose.com/2017/04/12/smug-illegal-alien-trashes-trump-live-tv-not-laughing-moments-later/#comments\">18 Comments</a></span> </p></header><div class=\"entry-content\" itemprop=\"text\"><div class='code-block code-block-5' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center;'>\n<script type=\"text/javascript\" src=\"//ap.lijit.com/www/delivery/fpi.js?z=403625&#038;u=chesclyde&#038;width=300&#038;height=250\"></script></div>\n<p>After her father and brother were detained by Immigrations and Customs Enforcement (ICE), an illegal alien decided to trash Donald Trump on live television. Unfortunately for the smug punk, things would go horribly wrong \u2013 and she wasn\u2019t laughing after what happened just moments after the cameras shut off.</p>\n<p>Daniela Vargas, 22, was furious to learn that the criminal actions of her father had finally caught up with him when he was arrested by ICE. Of course, seeing how federal agents also took her brother into custody at the time only made things worse, prompting her to announce a televised conference that she would be holding.</p>\n<blockquote><p>\u201cThe path to citizenship is necessary for DACA recipients but also for the other 11 million undocumented people with dreams,\u201d she said. \u201cToday, my father and brother await deportation while I continue to fight this battle as a Dreamer to help contribute to this country, which I feel that is very much my country.\u201d</p></blockquote>\n<p>However, the entitled punk quickly learned that you don\u2019t get everything that you want in this life, especially when you try to obtain it illegally.</p>\n<p>In fact, after trashing Trump and saying that those who broke the law should be rewarded, it wasn\u2019t long before officials heard what she had to say. Even better yet, the once smug and boldly outward illegal alien wasn\u2019t laughing just moments after her conference had ended. According to reports, ICE swept her up and is set to deport her as well:</p>\n<blockquote><p>ICE confirmed Vargas is in custody, \u201cUS Immigration and Customs Enforcement (ICE) took Daniela Vargas, 22, an unlawfully present Argentinian citizen, into custody March 1, during a targeted immigration enforcement action in Jackson, Mississippi.\u201d [Source: CNN]</p></blockquote>\n<p>It\u2019s honestly funny to see these morons keep showing their faces in some ill-founded act of protest only to get arrested. Even better yet, their so-called \u201cbrave\u201d action only results in these punks getting shipped back to where they came from.</p>\n<p>At this point, it\u2019s as simple as this; if you don\u2019t want to get deported, then don\u2019t break the law. The fact that people find this reality \u201cshocking\u201d is a disturbing indication of how little regard the former president had for the American judicial system. Justice is back \u2013 and it\u2019s about dang time.</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://madworldnews.com/illegal-alien-trashes-trump-tv/\"><em>h/t: madworldnews</em></a></p>\n<div class='code-block
